 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02.&nbsp;&nbsp; Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:6%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In accordance with Item&nbsp;2.02 of Form 8-K of the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;), Wal-Mart
Stores, Inc., a Delaware corporation (the &#147;Company&#148;), is furnishing to the SEC a press release that the Company will issue on August&nbsp;16, 2012 (the &#147;Press Release&#148;). The Press Release will disclose information regarding the
Company&#146;s results of operations for the three months and six months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 and the Company&#146;s financial condition as of July&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:6%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Press Release provides information regarding certain financial measures that may be considered non-GAAP financial
measures (each, a &#147;Non-GAAP Measure&#148;) under the rules of the SEC. Those Non-GAAP Measures include: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company&#146;s free cash flow for the six-month periods ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 and 2011, calculated as set forth in the Press Release (the
&#147;Free Cash Flow&#148;). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company&#146;s return on investment for the trailing twelve-month periods ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 and 2011, calculated as set forth in the Press
Release (&#147;ROI&#148;). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company&#146;s consolidated net sales and consolidated operating income and the Company&#146;s Walmart International operating segment&#146;s net
sales and operating income, in each case for the three months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 and stated on an adjusted constant currency basis calculated as set forth in the Press Release, the increases in such constant currency measures over the
corresponding reported measures for the three months ended July&nbsp;31, 2011 and the Company&#146;s consolidated net sales for the three months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 without the impact of the period-over-period fluctuations in currency exchange
rates (the &#147;Constant Currency Measures&#148;). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company&#146;s total U.S. comparable store sales and the comparable club sales of the Company&#146;s Sam&#146;s Club operating segment
(&#147;Sam&#146;s Club&#148;) for the thirteen-week and twenty-six week periods ended July&nbsp;27, 2012 and July&nbsp;29, 2011, projected comparable club sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the thirteen weeks ending October&nbsp;26, 2012 and comparable
club sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the thirteen weeks ended October&nbsp;28, 2011, in each case calculated by excluding Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s fuel sales for such periods (the &#147;Comparable Sales Measures&#148;). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The net sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 (the &#147;Subject Quarter&#148;) and the percentage increase in the net
sales and operating income of Sam&#146;s Club for the Subject Quarter over the net sales and operating income of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months ended July&nbsp;31, 2011, in each case excluding Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s fuel sales for the relevant
period (the &#147;Sam&#146;s Club Measures&#148;). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:6%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Press Release sets forth the reasons
why management of the Company believes the Free Cash Flow, ROI and the Constant Currency Measures provide useful information to investors regarding the Company&#146;s financial condition and results of operations. The Company&#146;s management
believes that the presentation of the Comparable Sales Measures and the Sam&#146;s Club Measures provides useful information to investors regarding the Company&#146;s financial condition and results of operations because that information permits
investors to understand the effect of the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club, which are affected by the volatility of fuel prices, on the Company&#146;s total U.S. comparable store sales, on Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s comparable club sales and on Sam&#146;s
Club&#146;s net sales and operating income for the periods presented. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01.&nbsp;&nbsp; Financial Statements and Exhibits.
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:3%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Exhibit 99.1&#151;A copy of the Press Release being furnished pursuant to the foregoing Item&nbsp;2.02 is
included herewith as Exhibit 99.1. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="4"><B>Company raises full-year EPS guidance; </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="4"><B>Walmart U.S. delivers fourth consecutive quarter of positive comps </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B><I><U>Q2 Highlights</U>:
</I></B></FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I></I></FONT>
<I></I></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (Walmart) reported second quarter diluted earnings per share from continuing operations of $1.18, at the top of our guidance of $1.13 to
$1.18. This was an 8.3 percent increase from the $1.09 per share reported for the second quarter last year. </I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>Walmart raised and narrowed full-year EPS guidance to a range of $4.83 to $4.93, from a previous range of $4.72 to $4.92. </I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>Walmart U.S. comparable store sales rose 2.2 percent in the 13-week period ended July&nbsp;27, with positive ticket and traffic. Walmart U.S. delivered its
fourth consecutive quarter of positive comparable sales. </I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>Sam&#146;s Club comparable sales, without fuel, increased 4.2 percent for the same 13-week period. </I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

approximately $2.2 billion. Without the currency impact<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">, net sales, which include

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>Walmart had free cash flow<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> of $6.1 billion for the six months ended July&nbsp;31. </FONT></I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I></I></FONT>
<I></I></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>Return on investment (ROI)<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> for the trailing 12 months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 was 18.1 percent. </FONT></I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>BENTONVILLE,
Ark., August&nbsp;16, 2012</B> &#151; Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (NYSE: WMT) today reported financial results for the quarter ended July&nbsp;31, 2012. Net sales for the second quarter of fiscal 2013 were $113.5 billion, an increase of 4.5 percent from
$108.6 billion in the second quarter last year. Net sales for this quarter included a negative currency exchange rate impact of approximately $2.2 billion. Without the currency impact, net sales would have been $115.7 billion. Membership and other
income increased 4.7 percent to $762 million. Total revenue was $114.3 billion, an increase of 4.5 percent from last year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><I><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP>&nbsp;</I></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><I></I>See additional information at the end of this release regarding non-GAAP measures. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">
 2
 </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Income from continuing operations attributable to Walmart for the quarter was $4.0 billion, up 5.7 percent from
the second quarter last year. Diluted earnings per share from continuing operations attributable to Walmart (EPS) for the second quarter of fiscal 2013 were $1.18. By comparison, last year&#146;s reported EPS were $1.09. The company had several
items last year that negatively impacted the second quarter by approximately $0.03 per share. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B><U>Strong earnings performance </U></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Walmart had a strong second quarter, and I&#146;m pleased with the earnings and overall results,&#148; said Mike Duke, Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. president and
chief executive officer. &#147;We had positive comp sales in Walmart U.S. and Sam&#146;s Club, as well as each of our International markets, reinforcing that customers rely on Walmart to help them save money and live better.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">The company leveraged operating expenses for the second quarter, delivering on its commitment to reduce costs, improve productivity and invest in price.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Our intense focus on delivering productivity initiatives and reducing costs allowed us to invest in lower prices for our customers and to deliver
strong profitability for shareholders,&#148; said Duke, who also highlighted the successful performance of the company&#146;s three operating segments. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;I&#146;m really pleased with the continued momentum in our Walmart U.S. stores, evidenced, in part, by three consecutive quarters of positive comp traffic
and four straight quarters of positive comp sales,&#148; Duke added. &#147;The team is very focused on delivering broad assortment and price leadership. Walmart&#146;s low prices drive greater customer loyalty. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Sam&#146;s Club had strong comp sales for the quarter. The quality and innovation behind merchandising and services are contributing to strong comps,&#148;
said Duke. &#147;The result of Sam&#146;s initiatives is greater value, which helps attract new members and strong renewals. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;We are also pleased
with the sales and profitability of Walmart International,&#148; Duke said. &#147;Our goal is to achieve more balance between profitability and returns, and we will do that by improving operational and sales productivity.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Duke also commented on the economic challenges facing customers. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;The paycheck cycle remains pronounced in the United States and in our International markets,&#148; Duke said. &#147;Given continuing economic pressures, we
believe that our price leadership and value are growing in importance to customers across income levels.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B><U>Returns </U></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Walmart delivered free cash flow of $6.1 billion for the six months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012, compared to $4.0 billion the previous year. Return on investment (ROI)
for the trailing 12 months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 was 18.1 percent, compared to 18.4 percent for the prior period. The decline in ROI is attributable to higher levels of average working capital, capital expenditures and the impact of acquisitions.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;We remain committed to providing strong returns to our shareholders,&#148; said Charles Holley, executive vice president and chief financial
officer. &#147;Walmart returned $3.1 billion to shareholders in the quarter, which included $1.3 billion in dividends and $1.8 billion in share repurchases.&#148; </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">
 3
 </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B><U>Company raises full-year EPS guidance </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;We take a variety of factors including sales trends, the global economy and currency into account in providing our EPS guidance. We expect third quarter fiscal 2013 diluted earnings per share from continuing
operations to range between $1.04 and $1.09. This compares to last year&#146;s third quarter reported EPS of $0.97,&#148; said Holley. &#147;We are raising and narrowing the company&#146;s full-year EPS guidance to a range of $4.83 to $4.93. Our
previous range was $4.72 to $4.92. Last year&#146;s full-year EPS was $4.54.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B><U>Operating segment details and analysis </U></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B><U></U></B><U>Net sales<B> </B></U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net sales, including fuel,
were as follows (dollars in billions): </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">The following explanations provide additional context to the above table for the second quarter. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"></FONT></FONT></TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Consolidated operating income, which includes unallocated other, was $6.7 billion, up 4.9 percent from last year. On a constant currency<I><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"></FONT></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> basis, consolidated operating income
would have risen 6.4 percent to $6.8 billion. </FONT></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS 2">&#151;</FONT></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"></FONT></FONT></TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Walmart U.S. operating income grew 5.3 percent for the quarter, outpacing net sales growth of 3.8 percent for the same period. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:30px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><I></I>See additional information at the end of this release regarding non-GAAP measures. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Walmart International&#146;s reported operating income increased 5.4 percent to $1.5 billion for the quarter. Constant currency<I><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> </FONT></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">operating income would have increased
11.9 percent to $1.6 billion for the second quarter. Currency exchange rate fluctuations negatively impacted operating income by approximately $110 million. </FONT></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">During the 13-week period, both comp ticket and traffic rose for Walmart U.S., and both grocery and general merchandise had
positive comp sales. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Our comp sales momentum continued through the second quarter, with July being one of our strongest months. All three
geographic business units and all store formats had positive comp sales. Customers are responding to our continued focus on providing the right assortment at everyday low prices and are shopping the entire store,&#148; said Bill Simon, Walmart U.S.
president and chief executive officer. &#147;We have a powerful strategy and I&#146;m confident in our ability to deliver sustained strong financial performance.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">For the 4-5-4 period from July&nbsp;28 through October&nbsp;26, Walmart U.S. expects comparable store sales to range from 1.0 percent to 3.0 percent. The Walmart U.S. 13-week comp for last year&#146;s third quarter
rose 1.3 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">For Sam&#146;s Club, comparable traffic and ticket, excluding fuel, increased for both Business and Advantage members for the 13-week
period ended July&nbsp;27. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Sam&#146;s Club had another impressive quarter, with positive comp sales from both Business and Advantage members. We
believe that the improvements in our quality and overall merchandise offerings are key to driving these results,&#148; said Rosalind Brewer, Sam&#146;s Club president and chief executive officer. &#147;Member engagement scores continue to achieve
record levels, and we&#146;re investing in price to deliver greater value to our members.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:30px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">
 5
 </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Sam&#146;s Club expects comp sales, without fuel, for the current 13-week period to increase between 3.0 percent
and 5.0 percent. Last year, Sam&#146;s Club comp, without fuel, for the third quarter comparable 13-week period rose 5.7 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Both Walmart U.S. and
Sam&#146;s Club will report comparable sales for the 13-week period on November 15, when the company reports third quarter results. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart Stores,
Inc. (NYSE: WMT) serves customers and members more than 200&nbsp;million times per week at 10,351 retail units under 69 different banners in 27 countries. With fiscal year 2012 sales of $444 billion, Walmart employs more than 2&nbsp;million
associates worldwide. Walmart continues to be a leader in sustainability, corporate philanthropy and employment opportunity. Additional information about Walmart can be found by visiting <U>http://www.walmartstores.com</U>. </FONT></P>

Information included in this release, including reconciliations, and the pre-recorded phone call are available in the investor information area on the company&#146;s website at www.walmartstores.com/investors. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">
 10
 </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Reconciliations of and Other Information Regarding Non-GAAP Financial Measures </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">(Unaudited) </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><I>(In millions, except
per share data) </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">The following information provides reconciliations of certain non-GAAP financial measures presented in the press release to which
this reconciliation is attached to the most nearly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). The company has provided the non-GAAP financial information
presented in the press release, which is not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as information supplemental and in addition to the financial measures presented in the press release that are calculated and presented in accordance with
GAAP. Such non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. The non-GAAP
financial measures in the press release may differ from similar measures used by other companies. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Free Cash Flow </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">We define free cash flow as net cash provided by operating activities in a period minus payments for property and equipment made in that period. Free cash flow was
$6.1 billion and $4.0 billion for the six-months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 and 2011, respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Free cash flow is considered a non-GAAP financial
measure. Management believes, however, that free cash flow, which measures our ability to generate additional cash from our business operations, is an important financial measure for use in evaluating the company&#146;s financial performance. Free
cash flow should be considered in addition to, rather than as a substitute for, income from continuing operations as a measure of our performance and net cash provided by operating activities as a measure of our liquidity. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Additionally, our definition of free cash flow is limited, in that it does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the
measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual obligations or payments made for business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental
information to our entire statements of cash flows. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Although other companies report their free cash flow, numerous methods may exist for calculating a
company&#146;s free cash flow. As a result, the method used by our management to calculate free cash flow may differ from the methods other companies use to calculate their free cash flow. We urge you to understand the methods used by other
companies to calculate their free cash flow before comparing our free cash flow to that of such other companies. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">The following table sets forth a
reconciliation of free cash flow, a non-GAAP financial measure, to net cash provided by operating activities, which we believe to be the GAAP financial measure most directly comparable to free cash flow, as well as information regarding net cash
used in investing activities and net cash used in financing activities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">
 11
 </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Calculation of Return on Investment and Return on Assets </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Management believes return on investment (&#147;ROI&#148;) is a meaningful metric to share with investors because it helps investors assess how effectively Walmart
is deploying its assets. Trends in ROI can fluctuate over time, as management balances long-term potential strategic initiatives with any possible short-term impacts. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">ROI was 18.1 percent and 18.4 percent for the trailing 12 months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012 and 2011, respectively. The decline in ROI is attributable to higher levels of average working capital, capital expenditures
and the impact of acquisitions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">We define ROI as adjusted operating income (operating income plus interest income, depreciation and amortization, and
rent expense) for the fiscal year or trailing 12 months divided by average invested capital during that period. We consider average invested capital to be the average of our beginning and ending total assets of continuing operations, plus average
accumulated depreciation and average amortization, less average accounts payable and average accrued liabilities for that period, plus a rent factor equal to the rent for the fiscal year or trailing 12 months multiplied by a factor of eight.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">ROI is considered a non-GAAP financial measure. We consider return on assets (&#147;ROA&#148;) to be the financial measure computed in accordance with
GAAP that is the most directly comparable financial measure to ROI as we calculate that financial measure. ROI differs from ROA (which is income from continuing operations for the fiscal year or trailing 12 months divided by average total assets of
continuing operations for the period) because ROI: adjusts operating income to exclude certain expense items and adds interest income; adjusts total assets from continuing operations for the impact of accumulated depreciation and amortization,
accounts payable and accrued liabilities; and incorporates a factor of rent to arrive at total invested capital. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Although ROI is a standard financial
metric, numerous methods exist for calculating a company&#146;s ROI. As a result, the method used by management to calculate ROI may differ from the methods other companies use to calculate their ROI. We urge you to understand the methods used by
other companies to calculate their ROI before comparing our ROI to that of such other companies. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">
 13
 </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">In discussing our operating results, we sometimes refer to the impact of changes in currency exchange rates that we use to convert the operating results for all countries where the functional currency is not the
U.S. dollar. We calculate the effect of changes in currency exchange rates as the difference between current period activity translated using the current period&#146;s currency exchange rates and the comparable prior year period&#146;s currency
exchange rates. Throughout our discussion, we refer to the results of this calculation as the impact of currency exchange rate fluctuations. When we refer to constant currency operating results, we are referring to our operating results without the
impact of the currency exchange rate fluctuations and without the impact of acquisitions until the acquisitions are included in both comparable periods. The disclosure of constant currency amounts or results permits investors to understand better
our underlying performance without the effects of currency exchange rate fluctuations or acquisitions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">The table below reflects the calculation of
constant currency for net sales and operating income for the 3 months ended July&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
